She is still crying day and night, forgetting to sleep and eat, and those who see it are all moved to tears. The headquarters has now sent the Deputy Adjutant's Office to cooperate with Wu Fan and the staff members to organize a funeral office, and the body will be put into the coffin at the hospital at 4:00 PM today (the 16th). (Evening of the 16th)

Appendix: Confession of the Suspect as Published in the Provincial Newspaper (Interrogator: ) What is your name? (Answer:) Feng Mingsheng, from Hengzhou, Guangxi, 20 years old, has a father, unmarried, has a younger brother, studied for three years. (Q:) Why did you assassinate Chairman Lü? (A:) In March and April this year, when I was in Luoba, Guangxi, Tan Qi, the attendant of Bai Chongxi, taught me to assassinate Chairman Lü. (Q:) Why did you assassinate Chairman Lü in Guangzhou? (A:) Tan Qi lived in Tai'an Inn. At 1:00 PM yesterday, he said to me, "Hurry up and take action, otherwise your name will be published in the newspaper, and you will be in trouble." I was forced by him, so I decided to commit the murder. (Q:) Where did you and Tan Qi discuss it? (A:) He and I discussed it in the kitchen of Tai'an Inn, and he told me to take action quickly. (Q:) Did you see him after 1:00 PM yesterday? (A:) After discussing it at the entrance of Tai'an Inn, he called a car to go with me. (Q:) Where is Tan Qi from? (A:) From Binyang County, Guangxi. (Q:) You must tell the truth and not implicate others. (A:) I am telling the truth. (Q:) After the incident, where did Tan Qi tell you to find him? (A:) In a boat in Shaqitou. (Q:) Did he definitely give you money to escape after the incident? (A:) He didn't give me any money to use. (Q:) How much money did he say he would give you after the incident? (A:) He promised to give me 10,000 yuan after the incident. (Q:) What is the name of the boat in Shaqi, and where is it berthed? (A:) I don't know the name of the boat. I remember that it was berthed under the dock bridge, and it was a boat for crossing the river. (Q:) When did you go to the boat with him? (A:) I went with him at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday. (Q:) How long did he take you to the boat, and what did you talk about? (A:) He urged me to start as soon as possible. There was also a mastermind who was a student at the Whampoa Military Academy. I don't know his surname. He had gold teeth. He was about twenty-five years old, of medium height. Someone told me that his surname was Liang and that he was also from Guangxi. (Q:) When did you see this Mr. Liang from the Whampoa Military Academy? (A:) I saw him the day before yesterday and today. (Q:) When did you see him the day before yesterday and today? (A:) The day before yesterday was at 3:00 PM, and today was in the afternoon. (Q:) Where did you see him? (A:) Tan Qi took me to see him at the Jinling Hotel.

Revised after

Regulations for Inspection of Imported and Exported Foodstuffs 66

In order to revise the regulations for inspection and registration of imported, exported, and transshipped foodstuffs, the National Government specially instructed the Executive Yuan, stating, "A letter from the Central Political Council was approved, stating that the Government Secretariat had previously forwarded the 'Regulations for Inspection and Registration of Imported, Exported, and Transshipped Grains' drafted by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining to the Central Political Council for consolidated review. The original document was copied and sent for verification. After being reviewed by the Civil Food Committee, it was reported that the draft regulations were generally appropriate, but there were still some articles that needed to be added or subtracted. After careful consideration and modification, a revised draft was prepared and submitted for review. As for the requests originally submitted by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining: (1) The inspection and registration of imported, exported, and transshipped grains should be handled by the Agricultural Products Inspection Institutes of the Ministry in Shanghai, Guangzhou, and other places, and entrusted to the municipal governments of Heilongjiang, Jilin, Liaoning, and Zhejiang provinces; (2) The Executive Yuan should order the Ministry of Finance to instruct the Inspectorate General of Customs to order all coastal customs offices that all imported, exported, and transshipped grains should be handled by customs officials who would notify the merchants to submit customs declarations, bills of lading, permits, and other relevant documents to the grain inspection and registration agencies for stamping, as a basis for assessment. These two points seem feasible, but since they involve implementation procedures, it is proposed that they still be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval and compliance. The 231st meeting of this council resolved that the revised regulations should be approved and the rest should be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval on file. Accordingly, the 'Regulations for Inspection and Registration of Imported, Exported, and Transshipped Foodstuffs' approved by this council are enclosed, and it is hoped that they will be followed for implementation and a response will be made. A copy of the 'Regulations for Inspection and Registration of Imported, Exported, and Transshipped Foodstuffs' is attached. Accordingly, it should be implemented immediately. In addition to instructing the office to reply, a copy of the attachment is hereby made and issued to the said Yuan for compliance."

Attachment: Regulations for Inspection and Registration of Imported and Exported Foodstuffs. (Article 1) The agencies responsible for implementing food inspection and registration are the Agricultural Products Inspection Institutes of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, or local agencies entrusted by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining. (Article 2) For all food imports, exports, or transshipments, the dealers or traders, merchants or companies, should first submit the customs declaration, bill of lading, permit, and other relevant documents to the local food inspection agency for stamping to certify registration. Regarding the food for which registration is requested in the preceding paragraph, the local food inspection and registration agency should send personnel to conduct on-site inspection when necessary. (Article 3) The seal used for food inspection and registration matters shall be issued by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining for the Agricultural Products Inspection Institutes and sent by the Ministry to the respective provincial and municipal governments for issuance to the entrusted agencies. (Article 4) Local food inspection and registration agencies shall implement the inspection and registration matters in accordance with these regulations, following the steps below in phases: Step 1: Rice, wheat, flour; Step 2: Other foodstuffs. (Article 5) All imported, exported, or transshipped foodstuffs shall be reported for inspection and registration before customs declaration. (Article 6) For imported foodstuffs that need to be sold urgently due to market demand or transshipped immediately for rapid transportation, the import and transshipment may be reported for inspection and registration at the same time. (Article 7) Merchants, companies, or firms that deal in or transport imported, exported, and transshipped foodstuffs shall report the following matters to the local food inspection and registration agency: (1) Name and address of the merchant; (2) Name and location of the company or firm; (3) Name, type, grade, quantity, and price of the foodstuff; (4) Place of origin and date of shipment; (5) Date of import, export, or transshipment; (6) Place of import, export, or transshipment and place of sale. (Article 8) The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining shall prescribe the format of the forms for the various items listed in the preceding article and issue them to the local food inspection and registration agencies for them to prepare and order the merchants, companies, or firms to fill out accordingly. (Article 9) Local food inspection and registration agencies shall compile statistical tables on a monthly basis from the date of inspection and registration and send them to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining for record. (Article 10) Local food inspection and registration agencies shall report the local food market prices to the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining for record on a monthly basis, and report immediately in case of special circumstances. (Article 11) When procuring food imports, exports, or transshipments, all agencies shall notify the food inspection and registration agencies of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining and the places of import, export, or transshipment, in order to facilitate inspection and registration: (1) Purpose of procurement; (2) Name, type, grade, quantity, and price of the foodstuff; (3) Place of origin and date of shipment; (4) Date of import, export, or transshipment; (5) Place of import, export, or transshipment and place of sale. The import, export, and transshipment registration agencies in the preceding paragraph shall, upon receiving the notice, first inquire by telegram with the agency in the import location that needs the foodstuff, obtain proof of their reply, and only release the foodstuff when the conditions are correct. After the foodstuff is imported, the agency in the import location shall still notify the inspection agency in the export location of the import and inspection situation. (Article 12) Food inspection and registration fees shall be waived uniformly. (Article 13) If local food inspection and registration agencies intentionally delay or engage in malfeasance, they shall be dealt with according to law. (Article 14) These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Wuhu Quick News 67

Fenglehe Town in Hefei, etc., had previously been robbed by bandits. Recently, Zhou Da Bay, Zhou Jia Wei, and other villages and towns in the northwest section of the county were attacked by more than 300 bandits. They first looted the guns from the group defense bureaus in the southern section of the west, killing several group defense soldiers. They then surrounded and looted Lei Ma Dian and other places extensively. According to a report from the Provincial Federation of Commerce, a telegram was sent to the provincial government requesting the dispatch of troops to suppress the bandits. Recently, a reply was received from the provincial government stating that a telegram had been forwarded to Wei Lihuang, commander of the Anhui North Bandit Suppression, to dispatch troops to suppress the bandits.

The Third Battalion of the Capital Garrison Regiment stationed in Wuhu captured a major thief named Tang Changhai outside the North Gate last night. He was executed by firing squad at the foot of Zheshan Mountain this afternoon.

A major fire broke out on Henan Weigeng Street at 1:00 AM this morning, and was extinguished after more than an hour. Nine stores, including Fusheng Kerosene Shop and Zhang Xingtai Grocery Store, were burned down, resulting in significant losses.

In the past, Qu Hongzhang and others organized a ferry company named "Tongji Company" for the counties of Hanshan and other counties north of the Yangtze River. The small ferry service has been operating for more than a month, which is convenient for travelers. Unexpectedly, many workers from the rowing industry gathered at the city party headquarters and municipal office to petition, claiming that the ferry service affected their livelihood. The city party headquarters immediately sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, ordering the ferry service to stop and await resolution. (18th)

Local Communications

Kunshan 68

The Fire Brigade Resumes Its Duties. Since the conflict between the fire brigades in various districts of this county and the former Public Security Bureau personnel during firefighting, the fire brigade members in various districts have not been dispatched when there were fire alarms for four days. Later, the directors of the fire brigades in various districts believed that this situation was not in the best interests of the local area, and immediately convened a meeting of all members to discuss the matter. They immediately resolved to resume firefighting duties to fulfill their responsibilities. The association convened a meeting of all members of the fire brigades in various districts of the city at 2:00 PM on the 20th at the public stadium to practice water pumping. The members had a group meal in the evening.

New Chief of Public Security Takes Office. The newly appointed Chief of the Kunshan Public Security Bureau, Qin Jieren, arrived in Kunshan at 3:00 PM on the 19th. After visiting County Chief Pang at the county government, he went to the bureau to take over his duties. It is heard that there will be changes in all internal departments.

Jiading 69

Adultery Case Sentenced to Imprisonment. Xu, from Dongxiang, had a small fortune. He married Zhang a few years ago. Zhang admired fashion and disliked her husband's ugly appearance. She was restless and came to the city to work as a nanny for a Chen family outside the West Gate. In February of this year, Chen dismissed her. She went to Ma Hu, who worked as a midwife on Beida Street, to ask for a recommendation. Ma's son, Qiu Quan, had been a widower for a while. Seeing that Zhang had a charming appearance, he kept her at home and allowed Qiu Quan to sleep with her. They had been together for more than two months. Recently, Xu learned about this and came to the city to investigate. He knocked on the door and entered the house, catching Ma Qiuquan and Xu Zhang together and sending them to the county for investigation. The case was handled by the new judge Zhang Yizhi. After repeated interrogation, the verdict has been issued, sentencing each to six months of imprisonment.

Burning of Opium. The county government had accumulated a large amount of opium and opium paraphernalia seized in previous cases since the time of former County Chief Ma. A detailed inventory had been prepared and submitted to the Civil Affairs Department and the High Court, requesting them to send personnel to jointly supervise the burning. The Civil Affairs Department commissioned Yuan Xiluo, the county chief of Taicang, to come to Jiading to supervise. At 2:00 PM on the 20th, the opium was burned in public in front of the county government hall.

Songjiang 70

Parade in Costume by Various Agencies. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the Provincial Itinerant Lecture Team, the County Party Headquarters, various agencies, and schools held a parade in costume. Representatives from various agencies and schools gathered at the County Party Headquarters and dressed up as designated characters, such as Feng Yuxiang, Yan Xishan, the Reorganization Faction, Communists, corrupt officials, local bullies, monks, Taoists, bandits, shamans, and witches. Some were the pests of society, while others were related to superstition. The costumes were exaggerated. The audience was as crowded as a wall along the parade route. After arriving at the Yue Temple, lectures were given at the Public Library. In addition to propaganda, the team's mission was to investigate various party and government matters and the hardships of the people, and then submit them to the province for solutions.

Opening of Bids for Demolishing the Moon City Announced. The County Construction Bureau plans to open up city street traffic and has submitted a request to the Construction Department to demolish the Moon City of the four city gates and solicit bids for the contract. Yesterday was the date for the opening of bids. As a result of the opening of bids, the bid of 605 yuan jointly submitted by Tang Zhongji, Zhang Xiangji, and Han Changbiao was selected. The second-highest bid was 195 yuan from Xie Hongji. Three days later, a guarantor will be sought to sign the contract with the bureau and start construction on schedule.

Fraud Case by Detectives. Detectives Li Yongde, Tang Shuqin, and Shen Ninglin of the County Public Security Bureau were ordered to be placed under surveillance by Chief Zhu of the Public Security Bureau on the 19th, and a document was prepared to transfer them to the county government for interrogation. According to the Public Security Bureau, the reason for the arrest was that Li and others had previously claimed to Hu Rongchu on Cangqiao Beach that the result of the tobacco investigation was that they had extorted hundreds of silver dollars, which were handed over at a certain hotel. Zhu Juken learned of this through inquiries and acted on the basis of a report from Ning, and then ordered the arrest. They are currently under detention by the county government for investigation.

Suzhou 71

Long-Distance Telephone Connections Between Nine Counties. Long-distance telephone connections between Wu County, Jiangsu, Wujin, and other nine counties have been established. The Provincial Construction Department has now decided to send personnel to Suzhou immediately to install the equipment. The plan is to install the equipment from Wujin to Wuxi, and then from Wuxi to Wu County, along the Lianhe River.

Accused of Being Reactionary, Declared Not Guilty. Ji Jiuyu, a member of the Standing Committee of the Provincial Nantong Middle School Student Association, was falsely accused of being reactionary in November of last year for opposing the principal. He was arrested and sent to the High Court. After repeated investigations by the court, it was found that Ji was diligent in his studies and cautious in his actions, and had no reactionary behavior. He was declared not guilty and released on the 19th.

Wuxi 72

Preparations for Receiving Wounded Soldiers. The Medical Department of the General Headquarters has determined that Huishan Mountain in Wuxi is the location of the 22nd Rear Hospital. The arrangements have been completed. The county government has also received a telegram from the Ministry of Military Affairs ordering them to quickly prepare for supplies. However, due to years of famine in Wuxi, reduced silkworm harvests, and the depression of all industries, the local finances are extremely depleted. Yesterday, a telegram was specially sent to the provincial government requesting that various expenses such as the supply and reception of wounded soldiers be disbursed from the provincial funds and reported for reimbursement upon completion. Furthermore, as the wounded soldiers will be transported to Wuxi soon, leaders of various agencies and organizations were convened to discuss protection and consolation matters. It was decided to establish three groups: General Affairs, Protection, and Consolation. The county government's Finance Bureau and Construction Bureau will be responsible for General Affairs. The Wuxi Gendarmerie Regiment, Water Police District, Public Security Bureau, and Business Corps will be responsible for Protection. The County Party Headquarters, Chamber of Commerce, Education Bureau, and various mass organizations will be responsible for Consolation. After the decision was made, each group convened separate meetings to discuss the specific measures. In addition, the General Headquarters organized a Wounded Soldier Management Committee, assigning various committee members to manage the wounded soldiers and all educational matters in various rear hospitals. Those assigned to Wuxi were Yu Zhihua as the team leader, and Cheng Zuwu, Cao Huan, Liu Tieshi, and Jiang Shi as team members. They arrived in Wuxi from Beijing yesterday to discuss all matters with County Chief Sun and Dean Cai.

Organization of Grain Inspection Office. In recent days, the price of rice has soared in Wuxi, making it difficult for the common people to obtain food. The county government has repeatedly received telegrams from the Department of Civil Affairs ordering the rapid establishment of a grain inspection office to prohibit private hoarding. Yesterday, a grain inspection office was specially organized at Daxukou to strictly inspect outbound grain. Wu Zhengrong, captain of the police brigade and water patrol team, was appointed as the director of the inspection, and Wang Zongzhi was appointed as the inspector. It was established immediately to prevent smuggling.

Investigation of False Accusation of Seduction and Abortion. The Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau outside the South Gate of Wuxi submitted a case a few days ago involving Hua Meichang's seduction of three young girls: Lu Aidi, Zhou Jinzhu, and Ding Zhangdi. The case was transferred to the county government for handling by the Public Security Bureau. After interrogation by Investigator Zhou, it was learned that the case was instigated by Lu Runchun (also known as Lu Yunzhong) from the South Gate, who falsely accused Hua Meichang of seduction in an attempt to harm him. The police were immediately dispatched to arrest Lu and bring him to the county, and the members of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Luo Xiaoda, were also summoned to the county for interrogation. Lu Runchun was evasive. In the second interrogation, Luo Xiaoda confessed, "I went to arrest the people based on Lu Runchun's report." Investigator Zhou said, "This case has been investigated clearly and is completely contrary to your report. You can still be forgiven if you tell the truth." However, Luo still refused to confess. After the interrogation, Lu Runchun was ordered to be detained, Luo Xiaoda was ordered to return, and Hua Meichang was released on bail. The three young girls were each taken back by their parents. It is heard that people in Nanli believe that the members of the Third Branch, Luo Xiaoda, were suppressing the facts and were particularly illegal. They will jointly submit a complaint to the Party and government authorities in the coming days, requesting that Bureau Member Luo be removed from office and punished.

Lu Jiumei Died from Abortion. Lu Jiumei (also known as Lu Ada), a 16-year-old maidservant in the home of Li Zhongchen, a resident outside the West Gate of Wuxi, had recently become acquainted with a certain Jia nearby, and became pregnant in secret. Jiumei went to the home of midwife A'erniang in front of Xiaomu Bridge for an abortion. Unexpectedly, the medicine was improperly used, and the fetus rotted in her abdomen. She was sent to Pu Ren Hospital for treatment, but the infection spread and she could not be saved. She died at about 1:00 AM on the morning of the day before yesterday. Her family reported the death to the county, requesting an autopsy. Yesterday afternoon, Investigator Yu went to conduct the autopsy and found that the deceased Lu Jiumei had indeed died from an incomplete abortion. After the autopsy, Yu instructed the deceased's mother, Lu Qian, to prepare a coffin and collect the body herself. Lu Qian had no money to buy a coffin, so Li Zhongchen provided the funds to purchase a coffin and collect the body.

Dispute Between Two Ferry Services Resolved. The Wuxi-Yixing and Wuxi-Suzhou ferry services in Wuxi had a dispute over the issue of starting the services, and could not reach a decision. Yao Dixing, Director of the County Construction Bureau, convened a meeting of the responsible personnel from both ferry services at the bureau yesterday. After discussion, the ferry routes and departure times were agreed upon, and the dispute was resolved.

Changzhou 73

Seizure of Illegal Gun Manufacturers. Xu Hongjin and Xu Dejin from Xiaoxujia Village near Zhengliuqiao Bridge in the Fifth District of Wu County hired ironworkers Xing Yuanlan and Jiao Laosi to manufacture guns at home. Gu Ben, the director of the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, learned of this and led a team of police officers to search the area on the morning of the 18th. They found an unfinished gun barrel, an old gun barrel, two firing mechanisms, and various other parts on the spot. The two workers were arrested. In the homes of Xu Hongjin and Xu Dejin, they found about 30 kilograms of iron materials and more than 30 pieces of iron files, iron hammers, and pliers, as well as a filing bed, a stone grinding bed, and a stove. However, Xu and others had escaped. The ironworkers confessed under preliminary interrogation that they had been hired to manufacture guns. They were transferred to the county on the 19th, and the county transferred them to the county court for interrogation.

Gendarmes Arrest Suspects. Gendarmes stationed in Changzhou went to various hotels to conduct inspections on the night of the 19th, accompanied by Tang Renjie, the director of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. In room 44 of the Jiqing Hotel on County Direct Street, they found Gong Baisheng, a traveler from Lianjiang Bridge. Inside his diary, there was a piece of paper with reactionary sentences. He was immediately taken to the Gendarmerie headquarters for interrogation along with He Guisheng, the owner of the hotel. In room 38 of the Dacheng Hotel in Gongjialong, they found Xia Zhiping, a native of Hunan, who claimed to be a platoon leader in the Second Division Training Regiment. He then claimed that his brother was working in the Chongfa Temple Corps, but he could not name the officers. More than one hundred silver dollars in five and ten dollar bills were found in his socks. Because his situation was suspicious, he was also taken to the Gendarmerie headquarters for interrogation.

Zhenjiang 74

Cooperative Trainees Assigned to Work in Various Counties. Cooperative business is a new emerging business in China. The general public, of course, does not know what it is. Even intellectuals and administrative officials often do not have a deep understanding of it. The central government issued a notice to the whole country, stipulating that the week starting from July 5th should be a cooperative movement promotion week. However, there is a lack of cooperative talent. Even if there are people who are enthusiastic about cooperative business, they are ultimately unable to reveal thorough theories and real benefits to awaken the public and achieve great results. Cooperative instructors have a considerable understanding and experience in cooperative theory and practice. Therefore, the Department of Agriculture specially dispatched cooperative graduates to various counties before July 5th to assist the Party and government in conducting large-scale propaganda and to make the public have a clear understanding so that they can automatically rise up and work hard in cooperative business.

Young Woman Saved from Drowning. At 8:00 AM yesterday, a young woman was about to drown herself at the ferry terminal on the riverbank. She was rescued by a police officer and survived. When asked about her name, she said that she was Xu Li, a native of Yancheng. She was abused by her husband at home, which led her to attempt suicide. The police officer sent her to the Women's Relief Center for temporary shelter.

Yangzhou 75

Establishment of an Office to Inspect Agricultural Products. Wheat transported and sold in various counties north of the Yangtze River often has cases of fraud. The Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Institute of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining learned of this and ordered Ge Jixian, dispatched by the Jiangbei Branch, to first set up inspection offices at key points such as Huojiaqiao Wharf to implement the inspection of agricultural products in Jiangdu County. The county received a consultation from Director Ge and took up his post at the wharf inspection office on the 16th. After taking the oath of office at a selected date, he will go to Huoqiao to set up an office to facilitate work.

Bandit Ship Attempts Robbery in Shaobo. Kongjiaqiao, west of the county-owned Shaobo Town in Xiyi, was suddenly attacked by more than 100 bandits on the late night of the 17th. They were riding in many small boats and were anchored on the river surface. The watchman there noticed and reported it to the Shaobo Public Security Bureau, the Business Corps, and the Water Police Team overnight. They immediately prepared for defense and the Business Corps and Water Police rushed to the scene, preparing to encircle and suppress them. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already heard the news and fled.

Chen Asks for Relief. A young woman came to the Women's Relief Center in the county yesterday evening (18th), requesting relief. After the center inquired about her origins, it was said that the woman was Chen Guizhen, 16 years old. She originally lived in the Yangzhou Church Ground, but her parents died early and her brother did not engage in legitimate work. A neighbor named Wang, seeing that she had no one to rely on, took her to Shanghai to work in a silk yarn factory. Initially, the woman only pocketed her wages. Later, seeing that the girl had grown up and was beautiful, she wanted to sell her to a brothel. The girl was deeply afraid of being trapped, so she fled back to Yangzhou alone. Unexpectedly, she could not find a single person who was an old friend or relative. In desperation, she turned to the Relief Center. Director Bao of the center has already kept her for education.

Jingjiang 76

Zhang Jiantang's Home Robbed. At about 3:00 AM on the morning of the 17th, multiple bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Zhang Jiantang in Zushidian, Second District, and broke open the door. Six people entered the room, wearing gorgeous clothes and speaking with local or Hebei accents. They first threatened the owner for silver dollars, and then looted clothes and ornaments worth about 300 silver dollars, as well as 40,000 copper coins.

Land Otterhead's Father and Son Kidnapped. Lu Yaoji and his young son from Land Otterhead, about three miles northwest of Gushan City in the Third District, were kidnapped by more than 20 bandits on the night before yesterday. Their neighbor Lu Shaoguan's son was also kidnapped, but was released after being taken a few miles north. The bandits have now instructed them to go to Hebei to negotiate the ransom.

Nantong 77

Planning the Merger of Tongtai Salt Fields. The salt production of the Tongtai salt fields in Huainan has been declining in recent years. Preparations are underway to merge the remaining Lusi salt field in. The Tongshu General Office of the Nantong, and the Taishu General Office of Dongtai, will also be merged. Another General Office will be established in a central location in Tongtai.

Bandits Arrested and Escorted for Questioning. The Fourth Brigade of the Provincial Police Corps arrested Qin Zhanzong, Wu Zhanlong, and Li Gan, three key criminals involved in the bandit case in Dongxiang, at the Huizhong Hotel in Tongcheng. Because the case was serious, they were escorted to the Temporary Bandit Suppression Command Post in Yuxi District for questioning.

Bandit Suppression Army Kills Bandit Leaders. The Provincial Defense Army fiercely suppressed the bandits claiming to be the Red Army in Hulong, Xinhe, and other towns. The Fourth Brigade killed the fake Commander-in-Chief Tang Chuyun and the fake Battalion Commander Qiu Jianzhong. The Zhang County Chief telegraphed the provincial government and the Civil Affairs Department on the 19th to report the details of the battle, and also telegraphed the Wusong Water Police District Department to dispatch shallow-draft warships to Nantong to intercept the fleeing bandits.

Director Dong Cables Request for Disciplinary Action Against Defense Lawyer. Dong Banggan, Director of the County Court of Nantong, was hearing a case of theft brought by Gu Guanru against Gu Yuanshi and Feng Yi on the 16th. The defense lawyer, Jiang Jue, requested the cancellation of the bail, which was not granted, leading to a dispute. Director Dong then sent a report to the President of the Jiangsu High Court stating that on a certain date, Banggan continued to hear the case of theft brought by Gu Guanru against Gu Yuanshi and Feng Yi. During the suspension of the hearing, the court instructed that Feng still be released on bail pending investigation. The defense lawyer, Jiang Jue, demanded that the bail be revoked. Banggan refused. The lawyer then incited more than one hundred spectators to applaud and curse, disrupting the order of the court. It is requested that he be disciplined according to law. Acting Director of the Nantong County Court and concurrently Judge Dong Banggan, Chief Prosecutor Zhu Ronggui, Judges Xu Lian, Li Wenwei, and Chai Zupeng, and Prosecutor Guan Junjie jointly sign and affix their seals.

Huzhou 78

Yongcheng Money Shop Grounded. Yongcheng Money Shop in the North Street of the city, opened in the spring of the sixteenth year of the Republic (1927), with a capital of 20,000 yuan. The manager was Shen Xiaokang from Shaoxing. However, the shop had little deposits. The loans it made were all withdrawn from Shanghai Ankang and other shops, and from various Jiangs in Suzhou. As a result, it made no progress. For three years, not only was there no official interest, but the expenses were still insufficient. At the end of last year, it was almost impossible to maintain. Fortunately, help from colleagues allowed it to survive the year. This year, the shop manager and Wang and others jointly opened a cocoon business. The cocoons they collected were mortgaged to Shanghai Ankang and Jiang, worth more than 200,000 yuan. When the accounts were settled, the shop owed Ankang more than 40,000 yuan in current accounts, which were all deducted. As a result, the shop's turnover was not working and it was grounded on the 15th. At that time, the manager, Shen Xiaokang, had returned to Shaoxing for business. Deputy Manager Xie Aitang telegraphed Shen to return to Huzhou. Shen rushed back the night before yesterday and was still thinking of ways to maintain it. However, the losses were too great and could not be recovered. It is heard that the manager and partners have 70,000 yuan in arrears, owe about 40,000 yuan to various shops in the city, 40,000 yuan to Shen shops, 80,000 yuan to various shops in Suzhou, and the total amount owed to depositors is no less than 200,000 yuan.

Jiaxing 79

Director of Education Bureau Accused of Dismissal. Ren Xuan, Director of the Jiaxing County Education Bureau, has been acting absurdly and has recently been accused of molesting a female staff member, causing much slander from the outside world. The Women's Association, the Student Union, the First District Party Headquarters, and the Xincheng Teachers' Union have successively listed the items and filed a complaint with the Education Department, requesting his dismissal and punishment. It is learned that the Education Department has already investigated and verified the matter and will transfer Ren to the province. Jiang Jingshuang, a graduate of the Jiangsu First Normal School, has been selected to succeed him.

Preparing to Reorganize Townships and Towns. The Jiaxing District Offices were all established on June 1st. Because the reorganization of townships and towns requires the separate merger or reduction of existing villages and neighborhoods, the district chiefs are currently planning the merger or reduction of each village and neighborhood. Mei Shouren, the chief of the First District, has already pre-approved the plan and, in accordance with the provisions of Article 37 of the County Organization Law, will convene a district affairs meeting of the villages and neighborhoods under his jurisdiction today (21st) to discuss the reorganization of townships and towns, so as to order the preparatory members to prepare for the implementation.

Ningbo 80

The Municipal Government's 200,000 Loan: Since assuming office, Ningbo Mayor Yang Ziyi has paid great attention to construction matters. It is now heard that the banking and financial sectors have approved the municipal government's 200,000 loan. With this loan secured, work can easily begin. The mayor has already instructed the Director of the Public Works Bureau to carefully plan the construction projects to be undertaken so that they can be implemented as soon as the loan arrives. It is also reported that the loan has been approved by the Bankers' Association after detailed discussions. However, the banking sector has not yet finalized the matter as there has been no contact. It is expected that after negotiations, there will be no problems. As for the members of the loan management fund committee, the number is still set at five, including Zhang, the Director of the Finance Bureau, Yang Juting, Lin Qinxiang, Chen Nanqin, and Zhou Zicai.

Chunhui Middle School Suspends Operations Due to Kidnapping Case: Zhang Yuwen, the head of general affairs at Chunhui Middle School in Yiting Baimahu, convened a meeting of the school board to discuss solutions after the school's principal, Fan Shoukang, teacher Wu Minxing, and student Xia Dingcai were kidnapped by bandits, resulting in no one to take responsibility for school affairs and students having no interest in studying. The meeting was held at the Jing residence in Baimahu at 2 PM on the 17th, with seven people including Jing Ziyuan in attendance. The results of the discussion were as follows: (1) The school will not pay ransom for the kidnapped Principal Fan Shoukang and others to prevent increasing banditry. The families of Fan and others must find their own way to rescue them. (2) Without effective security measures, no principal or teacher would dare to take the position and students, learning from the past, would sharply decrease for the next semester's school opening. Therefore, it was decided to temporarily suspend operations and submit the difficult-to-maintain reasons to the provincial government. If the provincial government has proper security measures for Baimahu, then the school will find a way to reopen. (3) The school closing date for this semester was originally July 1st, but now that people are anxious, the school will be dismissed early on the 19th. Each student, except for graduates, will be issued a transfer certificate.

Robbery Occurs at Fenghua Da Bridge: Wang, the sister-in-law of Dong Zhongxiu, a director of the Da Bridge in Fenghua, used to run the Dong Hengtai wine shop on the east bank of Da Bridge. After her husband went out to serve as an official, she closed the shop and moved to Rong Shili on the west bank. At 11 PM the day before, a bandit named Zhang Apin broke into Wang's home and forcibly robbed her of two gold rings she was wearing, injuring her finger. The suspect attempted to steal other items, but after she shouted for help, he fled with the rings.

Letter Received

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Police Headquarters 81

To the Editor:

Regarding the news item published in your newspaper on June 18th in the Jingjiang News column, "Provincial Police and Bandits in Fierce Battle," which stated that the defenses of Xilai Town were weak and that bandits intended to raid it. When Company Commander Wang Zhenwei learned of this, he immediately joined the Sixth Company to suppress the bandits at Yijiabao. Company Commander Wang set out at 6 AM on the 14th, but the Sixth Company failed to arrive due to unforeseen circumstances, resulting in insufficient government troops to fight the bandits. Company Commander Wang was hit by a bullet, soldiers were killed and wounded, and 21 firearms were lost. According to our investigation, all troops sent to various locations to engage in fierce battles with bandits are required to report the detailed situation to the headquarters afterward. However, we have not received any reports from the relevant unit regarding the events described in your newspaper. Considering the importance of suppression and the reputation of the military, we believe that your reporter's account is based on hearsay. Therefore, we have sent this letter to request a correction and kindly ask that it be published in the "Letters to the Editor" column.

Sincerely,

Jiangsu Provincial Police Headquarters

June 19th

Page 13

Local News: Finance Minister Song

Discusses the Closure of the Tianjin Customs 82

Background

Regarding the closure of the Tianjin Customs, Finance Minister Song, upon being asked for his opinion by a reporter from the Guomin News Agency, made the following statement: "A foreign adventurer, relying on violence, has dared to forcibly occupy the customs and openly threaten law-abiding Chinese customs officials with execution. Under these circumstances, the local customs authorities cannot perform their duties. Therefore, the National Government had no choice but to order the temporary closure of the Tianjin Customs. Judging from the current situation, this measure is both necessary and sound. Recently, Zhu Hexiang, a representative of the Northern warlords, declared to a Reuters reporter that the old tax rate of 5% ad valorem would be remitted as usual to pay foreign debts. In addition, the surcharges should be controlled by General Yan. As for domestic debts, most of them are secured by surcharges, and Mr. Zhu said that if these debts are not paid, Mr. Song should be held responsible. After the government ordered the closure of the Tianjin Customs, the pseudo-Tax Commissioner belatedly claimed that domestic debts should be paid on the same terms as foreign debts. In other words, the interests of domestic creditors suddenly received the same attention as those of foreign creditors in their minds. However, judging from their actions in destroying the customs system, it is clear that their claim to protect the interests of creditors is merely empty talk. The government is making every effort to correct the forced occupation of the Tianjin Customs, as this act, apart from the political implications, fundamentally undermines China's national credit. This move not only strikes a blow to domestic and foreign debts secured by customs duties, but also thwarts the government's repeated statements that it intends to reorganize the backward domestic and foreign debts. This year, it was originally planned to convene a meeting of creditors to discuss solutions, but this has also been affected."

The Tianjin Customs Incident

Difficulties for Shipping Merchants 83

Reduced Shipments to Tianjin

With the Tianjin Customs forcibly taken over by the North and Tianjin Customs duties collected, major public organizations in Shanghai have expressed their opposition. Even the staff of the Jianghai Customs have issued a declaration denying Xin Bosen as the Tianjin Customs Commissioner. Foreign merchants in Shanghai have also expressed strong dissatisfaction. The Finance Bureau has decided on a temporary solution to the Northern forced takeover of the Customs by ordering the Shanghai Jianghai Customs to collect the import half-tax that must be paid upon arrival in Tianjin, in addition to the export tax, for all shipments to Tianjin reported by various merchant guilds, starting yesterday (the 20th). The Customs has already issued a notice yesterday and started collecting the tax. However, the merchant guilds consider this to be a most difficult situation, as they are not allowed to refuse payment, but worry that when the goods arrive in Tianjin, they will be taxed again as in the Jianghai Customs example from previous years. Exporters are already discussing this issue.

Reduced Cargo to Tianjin: The amount of cargo exported from Shanghai to Tianjin this year has been minimal. Only in June did some textiles begin to be shipped, but this was only 20-30% of last year's business. Of the ships from Shanghai to Tianjin, foreign merchants' regular liners include six British ships and seven Japanese ships. There are only two Chinese ships. Yesterday, the Northern merchant guilds in Shanghai, fearing that they would have to pay double taxes on goods going to Tianjin, implemented a reduction in exports and temporarily tested shipments to Tianjin.

Temporary Ships Stop Going to Shanghai: Most of the temporary cargo ships going to Tianjin are British and Japanese. Recently, since the forced takeover of the Tianjin Customs, the shipping companies have found that the tonnage tax, which was usually paid in Shanghai and allowed ships to pass through all locations, is now also being collected in Tianjin. Moreover, most of these taxes are due at the end of June, with payment due in July. Yesterday, it was heard that in order to avoid the ship tax, the shipping companies have ordered the temporary cargo ships with expired taxes to stop sailing to Tianjin.

The New French Envoy

Mr. Wilden Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 84

Going to Beijing Next Wednesday

Date of Presenting Credentials Undetermined

Mr. Wilden, the new French Envoy to China, his wife, and his niece departed from Paris and arrived in China on the "Garoosha" passenger ship from Marseille to assume their new posts. They arrived in Shanghai at 8 AM yesterday morning. The French Consul-General, Mr. Cosserat, the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Chen Shiguang, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, and other Chinese and French officials greeted them at the Bund Wharf in the French Concession. From the Avenue Dubail Wharf to the French Consulate General's Office, French soldiers and Annamite constables lined up to welcome them. After landing, Envoy Wilden went to the French Consulate General's Office to rest briefly. The French Navy Band played military music to pay tribute. The new French Envoy and his wife then drove to No. 31 Rue du Kiang-Si to reside. This reporter also visited them. The room was filled with flower baskets presented by various sectors. Mr. Wilden is about 50 years old, energetic, and speaks fluent Chinese. When talking to the reporter, he asked about various matters in Chinese. Mr. Wilden will stay in Shanghai for about a week and is scheduled to leave Shanghai next Wednesday or Thursday to take up his post at the embassy in Beijing. Then, he will set a date to officially present his credentials in Beijing. The French political and business communities in Shanghai have scheduled a public banquet for Mr. and Mrs. Wilden at the Shanghai Club next Monday evening and at the French Club next Tuesday evening. Envoy Wilden served as the French Consul-General in Shanghai after the European War and previously served as Consul in Chengdu, Yunnan, and other places. He is quite familiar with Chinese affairs and has many old friends among the Chinese and French people here.

Photography of the New French Envoy Disembarking (Photo by Wang Xiaoting) 85

Chamber of Commerce Reorganization

Representatives' Congress Today 86

Starts at 9 AM

Total of 369 Representatives

The Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Congress is scheduled to start at 9 AM today with representatives from various industries in the city. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. The following is a record of yesterday's news.

Number of Registered Member Representatives: As of yesterday, a total of 142 industry associations with 346 representatives, and 18 store members with 23 representatives, have registered, for a combined total of 369 member representatives.

Today's Congress Agenda: In addition to electing the Executive Committee and Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, today's Congress agenda includes reading the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Charter and discussing nine important proposals, as well as other matters.

Allocation of Congress Staff: The allocation of duties for the Congress staff is as follows: (A) Presidium: In accordance with the Chamber of Commerce Law, all Standing Committee members will take turns serving and allocate duties, including (1) Reading the Premier's Will (Ye Huijun), (2) Delivering the Opening Remarks (Yu Qiaqing), (3) Reporting (Wang Yansong), (4) Discussing Proposals (Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong), (5) Reporting the List of Elected Executive Committee Members (Qin Runqing), (6) Reporting the List of Elected Supervisory Committee Members (Gu Xinyi), (7) Reading the City Chamber of Commerce Charter (Wang Xiaolai), (8) Delivering the Closing Remarks (Xu Jiqin). (B) Master of Ceremonies: Director of the General Affairs Section, Lu Fengzhu. (C) Discipline: Director of the Finance Section, Hu Xisheng; Director of the Guidance Section, Lu Wenshao; Director of the Investigation Section, Chen Songyuan; Director of the Registration Section, Zheng Chengqing. All other staff members will be divided into reception, counting, ushering, ballot counting, and tallying duties.

Exhibition Hall and Library Closed for Reading: The Commodity Exhibition Hall and Commercial Library attached to the Chamber of Commerce will be closed for reading this afternoon because all staff members must assist with the Congress affairs. It will be open as usual until noon. All staff members will also start working one hour earlier today, at 8 AM. The Chamber of Commerce has also sent letters to the Public Security Bureau and the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, requesting them to send police to take care of the large number of attendees and crowded vehicles.

Meeting of the Full Reorganization Committee: At 2 PM yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Committee convened its 14th full committee meeting, with 20 members in attendance. First, the entire Reorganization Committee took a group photo, and then the meeting was opened to discuss the following proposals: (1) Review of the qualifications of store member representatives. It was resolved to follow the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's instruction that businesses in the city with more than seven companies in the same industry cannot join the Chamber of Commerce independently and must wait until an industry association is organized before the association sends representatives to join the Chamber. The 28 companies that requested to join the Chamber were divided as follows: (A) The following 18 companies are allowed to join: (1) Longzhang Paper Mill, (2) Meihuali Clock and Watch Factory, (3) Zhufeng Enamelware Company, (4) Gengxin Stage, (5) Huashengrong Jade Store, (6) Securities and Commodities Exchange, (7) Scientific Instrument Museum, (8) Gold Exchange, (9) Yili Soda Factory, (10) Zhenhua Paint Company, (11) Jiangnan Paper Company, (12) Securities Exchange, (13) Industrial and Commercial Savings Association, (14) Tianchan Stage, (15) Huacheng Weaving Sailcloth Factory, (16) Yizhonghua Commercial Auction House, (17) Huizai Reclamation Company, (18) Tongyi Trust Company. (B) The following eight companies cannot join independently: (1) Weitong Yarn Factory, (2) Minsheng Yarn Factory, (3) Tongde Real Estate Company, (4) Hengyuanxing Flower Factory, (5) Jisheng Yarn Factory, (6) Yucheng Firm, (7) Yufeng Company, (8) Dafeng Company. (C) The following two companies are still under investigation: (1) Hongmei Firm, (2) Longtai Leather Cane Factory. The above three categories, totaling 28 stores, will have their membership applications suspended immediately before the Representatives' Congress. The membership applications of Feixing Tricycle Factory, Yapuer Electric Factory, Jingyi Tannery, and other stores will be handled in accordance with the regulations after the Member Representatives' Congress. (2) Discussion of handover methods. It was resolved that after the Executive and Supervisory Committee members of the City Chamber of Commerce are elected, the Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Committee will hand over its affairs. The Standing Committee is responsible for the handover.

Meeting of the Proposal Review Committee: At 2 PM the day before, the Proposal Review Committee of the Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting to review in detail the proposals submitted by various industry associations. The results were as follows: (1) One proposal from the coal industry regarding respecting the Law on Handling Labor Disputes and eliminating actions outside the scope of labor disputes was resolved to be submitted to the Congress. (2) Two proposals from the civilian shipping industry. (A) How to properly ensure protection when foreign ships damage Chinese ships in order to safeguard navigation rights was resolved to be submitted to the Congress. (B) Member resistance to paying monthly fees hinders the work of the association, and strict warnings should be given. The decision was made that the situation regarding the collection of monthly fees differs in each industry. It should be up to each industry to find its own way to reorganize and does not need to be submitted to the Congress. (3) Five proposals from the shoe industry. (A) What methods should be used to solicit industry members to join? (B) How to remedy difficulties in collecting membership fees? The decision was made that the above two proposals regarding membership fees and membership issues rely entirely on the sound development of chamber of commerce affairs, so that those who have not joined the chamber of commerce feel the benefits of joining the chamber of commerce, and difficulties will be readily resolved. It is neither enforceable by law nor can a proposal be created out of thin air, so it will not be effective, and there is no need to submit it to the Congress. (C) Urge the labor union to vacate the house. It was resolved that the Chamber of Commerce will send a letter to the Social Bureau to verify and there is no need to submit it to the Congress. (D) The illegal actions of the workers' union. The decision was made that the points mentioned are suitable for the degree of violating the police penalty law, so-called "inflicting violence on people, not to the point of injury," and should be handled from the administrative aspect. Both labor and management should respect the Law on Handling Labor Disputes, which has already been proposed by the coal industry. (E) The industry rules that have been approved for record should be followed by the industry. The decision was made to merge it with the same proposal from other associations and submit it to the Congress. (4) One proposal from the sausage industry. Non-member industry members should abide by the association's resolutions. The decision was made that the association's resolutions should not have a binding effect on industry members who are not members of the association. However, the nature of the industry rules approved by the competent authorities is different from the association's individual resolutions. Since they have been approved by the government, there should be no abuse of bias and monopoly. In order to protect the public interest of all industry members, non-member industry members have an obligation to comply, that is, to submit the original case to the Representatives' Congress after revision. (5) One proposal from the Western clothing industry. Transfer to Chinese weaving industry to improve weaving to be suitable for manufacturing Western clothing materials. The decision was made that the Chamber of Commerce should immediately transfer the letter to four industry associations: woolen fabric factories, electrical silk weaving factories, mercerized cotton weaving industry, and silk industry, without having to submit it to the Congress for discussion. The detailed method of promoting domestic products has been drafted by the association, and will be organized into a special committee after the City Chamber of Commerce is established to actively handle it. (6) One proposal from the department store industry and the pollen industry. The industry regulations approved by the association should be regarded as special regulations for the industry by the government, and non-member industry members should comply with them. The decision was made to submit the proposal from the sausage industry and the shoe industry to the Representatives' Congress. (7) One proposal from Wang Yansong, a representative of the silk industry, and Zheng Chengqing, a representative of the southern goods industry. Create a commercial school to train commercial talents. The decision was made to submit it to the Congress. (8) Two proposals from Luo Qinghua, a representative of the silk industry. (A) Industry association houses should not be arbitrarily occupied without the permission of the association.

Page 14

It was resolved to submit it to the Congress. (B) Should the workers' union exist? Please forward it to the central government for interpretation. The decision was made that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has clearly recognized that shop assistants are merchants in the interpretation of the Law on Handling Labor Disputes. The Union Law does not have the name of a workers' union. It should not exist legally. The Executive Yuan's instructions have been approved and the Ministry has informed the provincial and municipal governments. The original text has been published in various newspapers on the 18th of this month. The points mentioned in the proposal have been resolved and there is no need to submit it to the Congress for discussion. (9) Four proposals from the tea industry. (A) Association members should not be allowed to freely withdraw from the association, and they should not stop paying monthly donations. (B) At least one person from each industry shop must join the association. Non-members should have methods to be banned. The decision was made that restrictions on members joining and withdrawing from the association are inconsistent with the Ministry's interpretation of free duties and cannot be proposed for deliberation. (C) Industry members should abide by industry rules. (D) Industry members should abide by resolutions. Otherwise, a method of punishment should be stipulated. The decision was made to submit the proposal from the sausage department store industry and the pollen industry to the Congress. A total of 18 proposals were received from various associations. After the review, four proposals were submitted to the Congress alone, five proposals were submitted to the Congress together, two proposals were followed by the association, one proposal had been clearly explained by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and did not need to be discussed, and six proposals should be handled by each association on its own. There were a total of 18 proposals.

Municipal Government

Disputes Over Police Power on Boundary Roads 87

A letter to the American Consul-General and Leading Consul, Mr. Cunningham. Yesterday, the Municipal Government sent a letter to the American Consul-General and Leading Consul regarding the police power on the boundary roads, stating: "We have received your letter and understand its contents. The Municipal Government has always believed that the Shanghai Municipal Council's various measures on the boundary roads are unfounded in law and unreasonable in principle. Regardless of whether the 1899 Yangjingbang Land Regulations, which the Shanghai Municipal Council uses as an excuse, have been formally approved by the Chinese government, even according to Article 2 of the regulations, it can only obtain the right to purchase land within the restricted area. As for the right of security, it is originally the supreme power of the state and cannot be usurped or assumed by others. Since the boundary roads are Chinese territory and the routes pass through areas within the scope of this city, then the exercise of police powers by the police of this city on the roads cannot be regarded as outside the law or irregular actions. In response to the previous letter, we hereby reply for your information."

China and Foreign Powers Telephone Company

Calling a Shareholders' Meeting 88

Voting on the 25th

Meeting on the 27th

Share Transfer Suspended for Three Days

The Shanghai Hua Yang Telephone Company Limited addresses its shareholders:

Esteemed Shareholders,

We respectfully inform you that the declarations of April 26th and May 28th, 1930, along with the submitted bids from various companies to purchase the company's operations, which were attached to the second declaration, and the report from the advisory committee, have been duly reviewed. The directors must inform you that the Shanghai Public Works Department and the French Municipal Council have both approved the company's proposal to transfer telephone services to the International Telephone and Telegraph Company (ITT), and have agreed to grant them the exclusive rights. Therefore, a shareholders' meeting is scheduled for June 27th, 1930, to propose necessary resolutions so that shareholders authorize the company to accept the ITT's bid and transfer the company's operations to the new company. In this regard, the directors have revised the original terms of ITT's bid, making significant changes. The revised terms are listed below. This is a factual matter, and we urge you to pay attention:

(A) The capital invested by the new company in the business, as interpreted in the amended exclusive rights agreement, will have a net profit fixed at 8%.

(B) 2% of the capital invested in this business will be allocated annually to public bonds, up to a maximum of 20%.

(C) After the above two items have been deducted and allocated, any surplus should be divided equally between the new company and a revision of the fee pricing structure.

(D) Current user fees must not be increased until the telephone system is completely converted to an automatic system.

(E) Once the above conversion is completed, fees should be charged according to the prices proposed in Mr. An Sheng's report, in addition to the public contributions paid to the two Public Works Departments.

(F) After Mr. An Sheng's prices are implemented, they must not be increased for three years, but prices can be reduced.

(G) If, during the conversion to the automatic system and the implementation of Mr. An Sheng's prices, profits are insufficient, they cannot be recovered in subsequent years.

The directors earnestly recommend that the shareholders accept the ITT's bid, and we dare to state that in negotiating this matter, the directors and company executives have carefully considered and consistently taken into account the interests of both shareholders and users. The directors recommend accepting the bid and respectfully present the reasons for this recommendation, hoping that shareholders and users will carefully review them.

Esteemed Shareholders, regarding the issue of the old company's stock price, the board of directors has carefully considered it. The price ITT is willing to pay is either 75 taels of silver per share, or, at this rate, 1.5 shares of the new company's stock in exchange for one share of the old company's stock. Each shareholder is free to choose either option: whether to sell the old shares for cash at 50% above face value, or to continue participating in the new company's operations by exchanging one old share for 1.5 new shares. If shareholders accept the latter option, they can retain their interests in the new company, just as in the old company.

ITT has expressed its strong desire to have a larger number of people than currently enjoy the benefits of this business. The company's position, as an operator of public utilities, cannot regard the stock price as the sole criterion. A high price would require increasing capital, and the profits would need to be calculated based on the capital.

Esteemed Users, during negotiations with ITT, the directors and the company agreed that the price of fees must be maintained during the reorganization of the automatic system (for two years). After the reorganization, ITT has agreed to use the prices suggested by Mr. An Sheng as the basis for fees and has agreed not to increase these prices for three years. At the end of the three years, the issue of price increases should be handled according to the regulations on percentage profits.

The prices suggested by Mr. An Sheng are based on immediate implementation, while the above-mentioned method agreed upon by the directors and ITT ensures that the current low prices can continue for two years, and that the price increases proposed by Mr. An Sheng (which are still extremely low compared to other places in Shanghai) will be the maximum price for the following three years.

Finally, the directors wish to reiterate and request a review of the following points:

(1) ITT's bid is consistent with the company's previously announced strategy, and Mr. An Sheng also agrees with this strategy.

(2) The advisory committee recommended accepting ITT's bid, and the two Public Works Departments subsequently approved the bid.

(3) The bid allows for public service, ensuring rapid improvement and superior work, permanent maintenance, and constant addition of equipment to provide the public with a first-class telephone system.

(4) The company's development plans have been delayed for many months due to the need to examine other automatic telephone systems. Such delays have already caused significant losses. Further hesitation would have unthinkable consequences.

In view of the above points, we hope that the shareholders will support the directors' recommendation and vote in favor of the proposals at the meeting on the 27th. To ensure a sufficient quorum for the meeting and voting, we urge all shareholders who cannot attend to promptly fill out the attached proxy form and return it to the company by 4:00 PM on Wednesday, June 25th. This is our most earnest request.

With best wishes,

On behalf of the Board of Directors, Acting Chairman P. Bale, June 19th.

Another Notice to Shareholders:

This is to notify you that the Shanghai Hua Yang Telephone Company Limited will hold a special shareholders' meeting at 4:00 PM on Friday, June 27th, 1930, at the Royal Asiatic Society Hall, 5 Museum Road, to propose the following resolutions:

All the amendments to the ITT bid, as described in the letter from Mr. Keer, Vice President of ITT, to the Chairman of the Board of Directors of this company on April 15th, 1930, should be accepted, subject to any modifications deemed necessary by the directors of this company. Furthermore, the directors should be instructed to immediately transfer the company's operations to the new company mentioned in the letter and to sign and complete all necessary agreements and procedures to execute this matter. This is hereby proposed.

All of the company's transfer books and stock registration books will be closed from June 25th to June 27th, 1930 (inclusive). This is to notify all shareholders for their information.

By order of the Board of Directors, Secretary Lang Hexi Te, June 19th, 1930.

The Case of the Pharmaceutical Industry Placing Unemployed Workers

Finally Resolved Recently 89

Introducing Fifty People for Employment in the Pharmaceutical Industry

Those Who Do Not Qualify Will Receive a One-Time Severance Payment

Revised Conditions to be Handled by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The case of placing unemployed workers in the pharmaceutical industry in this city has been resolved by the full committee of the Chamber of Commerce. Yu Qiaqing, Ye Huijun, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, and Wen Lanting were publicly elected as five committee members to represent the industry and petition the Central Party Headquarters in Beijing to withdraw the order. This was previously reported in the news. We now hear that this case has been resolved. The details are as follows:

After the representatives of the petition returned to Shanghai from Beijing, they received Order No. 9393 from the Central Executive Committee, which stated: "Received. The labor-capital dispute in the pharmaceutical industry in your city has been prolonged and unresolved, which is inappropriate. The association should be allowed to select and introduce 50 qualified unemployed workers from the 128 eligible workers to the capital side for immediate employment. Regarding the elimination of the substitute worker system, many of the 13 articles previously agreed upon by the labor and capital sides of the pharmaceutical industry are inappropriate and also conflict with the Trade Union Law. After this case is resolved, the association should investigate and study it, and then submit it to the municipal party and government organs for proper revision to resolve the dispute. In addition to instructing the Shanghai Municipal Party Department and Municipal Government to investigate and handle it, you should also inform them of this order."

Employing Fifty Unemployed Workers. After receiving the Central Order, the association reported it to the Standing Committee for discussion and decided to comply. At the same time, it notified the National Pharmaceutical Industry Union to comply. The Municipal Government and Municipal Party Department also received the Central Order and instructions on how to handle it. The Chamber of Commerce then sent a letter to the Civic Training Association, requesting that the names, native places, and resumes of the unemployed workers be sent to the association for review and introduction. Subsequently, the association received a list copied by the Civic Training Association, totaling 128 people. After excluding those who already had jobs and those who had been expelled from the association for various reasons, there were actually 101 people. The 54th and 55th Standing Committee meetings of the Chamber of Commerce then decided to introduce 50 people from the list and issued a list to the National Pharmaceutical Industry Association to distribute to various stores for employment. The list of 50 people is disclosed below: 1. Mi Weixian, 2. Xu Dingtai, 3. Yu Xiaxian, 4. Guo Yuankang, 5. Wang Yongsheng, 6. Du Jiabin, 7. Li Meihua, 8. Wei Xiqi, 9. Hu Lianfang, 10. Dong Rusheng, 11. Zhang Jinbao, 12. Shi Shanxiao, 13. Zhang Huaqing, 14. Yang Guobin, 15. Zhu Dongchen, 16. Yu Tianzhu, 17. Yu Bangheng, 18. Zhang Zhenhui, 19. Gao Bingsheng, 20. Chen Yunbao, 21. Fei Fugeng, 22. Nie Jichang, 23. Sun Yunxia, 24. Zheng Xizhou, 25. Shen Jinsheng, 26. Fang Fusheng, 27. Gu Jinfa, 28. Qiu Wangzhou, 29. Liu Songjun, 30. Wang Xiangjun, 31. Yang Liansheng, 32. Feng Yongyuan, 33. Sun Kaiyuan, 34. Zhao Xinan, 35. Yang Xuewei, 36. Chen Shanzhang, 37. Lv Nansheng, 38. Zhou Yaseng, 39. Wu Liangquan, 40. Fang Lusheng, 41. Zhu Bingjiang, 42. Zhu Yuanlin, 43. Gao Meiqing, 44. Gu Meixuan, 45. Wang Yongcai, 46. Chen Jinzhang, 47. Bian Zucheng, 48. Shi Chunhui, 49. Li Huaifang, 50. Xia Qinsheng.

Those Who Do Not Qualify Receive Severance Pay. For the 51 workers who were previously reviewed and found unqualified by the party and government organs (in addition to the 128 people), according to the decision of the central and municipal party and government organs, each person was given 20 yuan for travel expenses to return to their hometown, totaling 1,020 yuan for 51 people. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce sent the full amount to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for distribution.

Revised Conditions Transferred to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. Regarding the pharmaceutical industry employee treatment conditions that conflict with the Chamber of Commerce Law and the Trade Union Law, according to the Central Order, the Chamber of Commerce should review and discuss revisions, and simultaneously resolve the substitute worker system and the apprentice promotion system. Because the Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to convene a city-wide representative conference today to prepare for the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, it is not possible to handle it in time. The 55th Standing Committee meeting decided to transfer it to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce to continue to comply with the Central Order.

Reporting the Handling Process to the Central Government. The Chamber of Commerce reported to the Central Government yesterday on the handling of this case in compliance with the order, and the transfer of the revised conditions to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for record-keeping.

Local News: Picking Up Shell Casings

Tragic Incident of Shell Casings Exploding and Injuring Many People 91

Zhou Zhenqian Discarded Shell Casings

Scavengers Gathered to Collect Them

Unexpended Powder Remained in the Shell Casings

A Loud Explosion Led to a Major Disaster

Zhou Zhenqian, a Shandong native, has been running the Sanhe Yong Waste Copper Tin Shop at Liu's Tomb Alley in Qinglian Street, Nine Mu Di, Nanshi. He specializes in collecting various types of copper and tin, melting them down, and then re-manufacturing various utensils. A few days ago, he suddenly bought more than 80 kilograms of discarded shell casings. When he bought them, Zhou thought the shell casings were made of copper. Unexpectedly, when he attracted them with a magnet, more than 50 kilograms of them were made of copper-clad iron. If copper and iron are melted in the same furnace, the pure copper will be useless. Therefore, Zhou was extremely frustrated afterward and threw more than 50 kilograms of iron casings into the trash can next to Xiong Changfa's wooden shop in Qinglian Street. Unexpectedly, many nearby scavengers saw Zhou throw out so many shell casings and thought they were valuable. They jointly pulled them out of the trash can and gathered on the side of the road to collect them. Unexpectedly, some of the shell casings still had unexpended powder. Due to excessive knocking, they suddenly exploded with a loud bang, alarming the surrounding area. As a result, seven people's faces were injured and they fell to the ground. Fortunately, nearby police officers heard the noise and rushed to the scene. They immediately reported the incident to the First Precinct of the Second District. Upon hearing the news, Chief Qian immediately led several senior police officers to the scene for a detailed inspection. He first inquired about the names of the seven injured people: Wang Youfa, 38 years old, from Zhenjiang, resident of No. 46 Qinglian Street, sustained injuries to three areas: face, chest, and legs; Tang Xilin, 33 years old, from Shaoxing (address unknown); Wang Simin, 22 years old, from Ningbo, resident outside Xiaobeimen; Lu Adu, local, 24 years old, resident of No. 14 Jiu Mu Di; and pedestrian Yan Dengshan, 44 years old, from Shandong, injured face. The above five people sustained face injuries, but were not seriously injured. Lu Awei, 30 years old, from Ningbo, resident of No. 40 Qinglian Street, sustained injuries to three areas: face, chest, and legs. His condition was the most serious and his life may be in danger. After the investigation, Chief Qian ordered several senior police officers to send the seven injured people to Renji Hospital. Because the hospital's wards were insufficient, four people were sent to Shanghai Hospital. He also took Shen Shiyou (23 years old, from Shandong), a partner of Sanhe Yong Copper Tin Shop, to the police station for questioning. He will submit a report along with the more than 50 kilograms of discarded shell casings to the Judicial Section for review.

Fu Ning Released from Prison This Morning 92

Following Cacia to Freedom

Following Cacia last autumn, Fu Ning, who was convicted of privately opening a roulette gambling den, also ran a gambling den called Fu's Gambling Cave at No. 5 Tongfu Road. He was sentenced to the same punishment as Cacia. However, the verdict was slightly later, so he was not able to be released at the same time as Cacia. Today, Fu's sentence has also been completed. Fu was released from the Xiamen Road West Prison at 8:00 AM this morning.

What a Coincidence

Matters Between Men and Women 93

Both Women are Pregnant

They Can Only Be Allowed to Get Married

Mei Xiaoyun. Mei Yunfu, a resident of No. 37 Sanyi Road, Wusong, is over 50 years old and still worried about having no son. He married a wife surnamed Li, who gave birth to a daughter named Xiaoyun, who is 18 years old and has a passable appearance. Last spring, through an introduction from a neighbor, she entered the spinning department of the Huafeng Yarn Factory in Yunzao Port, Wusong. Within a few months, she was seduced by Zou Zhichen, a staff member of the same department. Xiaoyun's love bud opened, and seeing Zou's youthful charm, she was completely captured by him. The two had already made mountains and sea oaths and agreed to stay together until they turned grey. Later, Zou thought that their relationship would not last long without a formal union, so he asked someone to mediate with Xiaoyun's father. Unexpectedly, many good things were frustrated, and he was severely rejected by Mei Yunfu. Xiaoyun knew her father's persistence, so she eloped with Zou like Hongfu and built another love nest. Within a few months, she was already pregnant. Her father found out. Because his beloved daughter had already made it a fait accompli, and publicizing it would affect his reputation, he automatically asked someone to mediate with Zou yesterday, willing to recognize him as his son-in-law and hold a wedding ceremony to make them a family.

Zhao Yinbao. Zhao Jiang, a local woman residing at Gaomu Bridge, east end of Lujia Du, Pudong, is 50 years old and has a daughter named Yinbao, who is 19 years old and not yet married. She works in the box-packing room of the Rongchang Match Factory in Lujia Du. Shi Xiaoqing, a 26-year-old worker from Qingjiang in the same factory, who had not yet married, had a love affair with Yinbao. They often secretly met and made a secret agreement to grow old together. Her mother did not know about it. Unexpectedly, on March 1st of this year, Yinbao suddenly disappeared. After many days, she had not returned home. Jiang was panicked and sent people to inquire everywhere. Until the afternoon of the 17th, she found out that she had been abducted by Shi. Jiang was furious and took Shi to the Third District Public Security Bureau, ordering him to hand over Yinbao. According to Shi Xiaoqing's confession, he admitted that he was in love with Yinbao. At the same time, Yinbao also confessed that she was willing to marry Shi. Even if Shi became a beggar in the future, she was willing to beg with him. They were both sent to the local court for disposal. The court, considering that the case involved the abduction of a young girl, instructed Jiang to file a separate lawsuit. Therefore, both parties left the court together at the time. However, Yinbao's relationship with Shi started last year, so she is now five or six months pregnant. Jiang thought it was a fait accompli and did not want to be involved in litigation. After mediation by a third party, it has been peacefully resolved. Yinbao has officially become Shi's wife, and the lovers have become a family.
